create table DECISIONINFO (
	DECISION_ID INT,
	USER_ID INT,
	DATE_CREATED VARCHAR2(10),
	WINNER VARCHAR2(1),
	WIN_PERCENT INT,
	COMPLETE VARCHAR2(5),
	PRIVACY VARCHAR2(7),
	STAR INT
);

--PRIMARY KEYS
ALTER TABLE USERINFO
ADD CONSTRAINT USER_ID_PK PRIMARY KEY (USER_ID);

ALTER TABLE DECISIONINFO
ADD CONSTRAINT DECISION_ID_PK PRIMARY KEY (DECISION_ID);

ALTER TABLE TITLE
ADD CONSTRAINT TITLE_ID_PK PRIMARY KEY (TITLE_ID);

ALTER TABLE CHOICE
ADD CONSTRAINT CHOICEDETAIL_ID_PK PRIMARY KEY (CHOICEDETAIL_ID);

--FOREIGN KEYS
ALTER TABLE DECISIONINFO
ADD CONSTRAINT USER_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (USER_ID)
REFERENCES USERINFO(USER_ID);

ALTER TABLE TITLE
ADD CONSTRAINT TITLE_DECISION_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (DECISION_ID)
REFERENCES DECISIONINFO(DECISION_ID);

ALTER TABLE CHOICE
ADD CONSTRAINT CHOICE_DECISION_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (DECISION_ID)
REFERENCES DECISIONINFO(DECISION_ID);
